Set-Content .\\utils\\logger.py -Encoding UTF8\n\n# === strategies/moving_average.py ===\n@'\nfrom statistics import mean\n\nclass MovingAverageStrategy:\n    \"\"\"\n    ì•„ì£¼ ë‹¨ìˆœí•œ ë°ëª¨ ì „ëµ:\n    - ë‹¨ê¸°/ì¥ê¸° ì´ë™í‰ê·  êµì°¨ë¡œ buy/sell/hold ê²°ì •\n    \"\"\"\n    def __init__(self, short: int = 5, long: int = 20):\n        if short >= long:\n            raise ValueError(\"shortëŠ” longë³´ë‹¤ ì‘ì•„ì•¼ í•©ë‹ˆë‹¤.\")\n        self.short = short\n        self.long = long\n\n    def signal(self, prices: list[float]) -> str:\n        if len(prices) < self.long:\n            return \"hold\"\n\n        short_ma = mean(prices[-self.short:])\n        long_ma  = mean(prices[-self.long:])\n\n        if short_ma > long_ma * 1.001:\n            return \"buy\"\n        elif short_ma < long_ma * 0.999:\n            return \"sell\"\n        return \"hold\"\n'@ | Set-Content .\\strategies\\moving_average.py -Encoding UTF8\n\n# === def signal(self, prices: list[float]) -> str:\r\n        if len(prices) < self.long:\r\n            return \"hold\"\r\n\r\n        short_ma = mean(prices[-self.short:])\r\n        long_ma  = mean(prices[-self.long:])\r\n\r\n        if short_ma > long_ma * 1.001:\r\n            return \"buy\"\r\n        elif short_ma < long_ma * 0.999:\r\n            return \"sell\"\r\n        return
